   rūpāṇyuditāni /	rUpANi-uditAni /
   amunā vāyunāyaṃ keśave viṣaye granthaḥ kṛta ityanvayaḥ /	amunA vAyunA-ayam keSave vizaye granTaH kRtaH iti-anvayaH /
   kīdṛśaṃ tasya mūlarūpaṃ kathaṃbhūtāni ca tāni trīṇi rūpāṇītyata uktam-	kIdRSam tasya mUla-rUpam kaTaMBUtAni ca tAni trINi rUpANi-iti-atas uktam-
   baḍityādi //	baxityAdi //
   yasya tanmūlarūpaṃ baṭ balātmakaṃ darśataṃ jñānarūpaṃ ca /	yasya tad-mUla-rUpam baj bala-Atmakam darSatam jQAna-rUpam ca /
   dṛśerauṇaśadiko 'tacpratyayaḥ /	dRSerONa-SadikaH atad-pratyayaH /
   anena vāyuśabdo niruktaḥ /	anena vAyu-SabdaH niruktaH /
   vaśabdo balavācī /	vaSabdaH bala-vAcI /
   ayatiḥ gatyarthaḥ /	ayatiH gati-arTaH /
   gatyarthāścāvagatyarthāḥ /	gati-arTAH-ca-avagati-arTAH /
   tata uṇ /	tatas uj /
   vaścāsau āyuśceti vāyuriti /	vaH-ca-asO AyuH-ca-iti vAyuH-iti /
   kiñca bhargo bharaṇagamanayoḥ kartṛ /	kiQca BargaH BaraNa-gamanayoH kartR /
   hubhṛñ bharaṇe, gamḷ gatau, ābhyāmasunpratyayo ḍicca /	huBRn BaraNe, gam? gatO, AByAm-asunpratyayaH xit-ca /
   idamapi vāyuśabdavyākhyānam /	idam-api vAyu-Sabda-vyAKyAnam /
   vā gatigandhanayorityataḥ kṛvāpājimisvadisādhyaśūbhya uṇityuṇ /	vA gati-ganDanayoH-iti-atas kRvApa-ajimi-svadi-sADya-SUByaH uNiti-uj /
   anekārthatvāddhātūnāṃ vātirbharaṇe 'pi vartate /	aneka-arTa-tvAt-DAtUnAm vAtiH-BaraNe api vartate /
   api ca mahat śreṣṭham /	api ca mahat SrezWam /
   vayaḥ śreṣṭhatva ityasmāduṇ /	vayaH SrezWa-tvaH iti-asmAt-uh /
   na kevalaṃ mūlarūpamevaṃ kintu yasyāvatāreṣu nihitaṃ rūpamitthameva /	na kevalam mUla-rUpam-evam kintu yasya-avatArezu nihitam rUpam-itTam-eva /
   yasya prathamakaṃ prathamaṃ rūpaṃ rāmaviṣayāṇi vacāṃsi mūlarāmāyaṇādīni	yasya praTamakam praTamam rUpam rAma-vizayANi vacAMsi mUla-rAmAyaNa-AdIni
   rāmavacāṃsi teṣāṃ nayaṃ nīyante śiṣyeṣu pravartyante 'neneti /	rAma-vacAMsi tezAm nayam nIyante Sizyezu pravartyante anena-iti /
   erajityac /	erajityat /
   yasya dvitīyaṃ vapuḥ pṛkṣaḥ /	yasya dvitIyam vapuH pRkzaH /
   pṛcchabdaḥ pṛtanāvācī prasiddhaḥ /	pRd-CabdaH pRtanA-avAcI prasidDaH /
   tasminkarmaṇyupapade kṣai kṣaya ityetasmāt āto 'nupasarge ka iti kaḥ /	tasmin-karmaNi-upapade kzEH kzayaH iti-etasmAt AtaH anupasarge kaH iti kaH /
   upapadatakāralopaśchāndasaḥ /	upapadata-kAra-lopaH-CAndasaH /
   puṃliṅgaṃ(ṅgaḥ) ca śrutyanusāreṇa /	puMliFgaM(FgaH) ca Sruti-anusAreNa /
   asunvā pratyayaḥ /	asunvA pratyayaH /
   kidita napuṃsakamevedam /	kidita napuMsakam-eva-idam /
   ripupṛtanākṣayakārītyarthaḥ /	ripu-pRtanA-kzaya-kArI-iti-arTaH /
   yasya tṛtīyaṃ vapuḥ etanmadhvaḥ /	yasya tRtIyam vapuH etat-maDvaH /
   madhuśabdaḥ sukhavācī /	maDu-SabdaH suKa-vAcI /
   "madhuta dyaurastu naḥ pitā'; iti prayogāt /	"maDuta dyOraH-tu naH pitA-a; iti prayogAt /
   vaśabdaḥ śāstrāparaparyāyatīrthavācī /	vaSabdaH SAstra-apara-paryAya-tIrTa-vAcI /
   vāteravagatyarthātkaraṇe ghañarthe kavidhānamiti kaḥ /	vAteH-avagati-arTAt-karaNe GaQarTe kaviDAnam-iti kaH /
   sukhasādhanaṃ tīrthamasyeti /	suKa-sADanam tIrTam-asya-iti /
   svarityatrevokāralopaḥ /	svariti-atra-ivokAra-lopaH /
   bhagavatsvarūpapratipādanenaiva granthopasaṃhāraḥ samucita	Bagavat-svarUpa-pratipAdanena-eva granTa-upasaMhAraH samucita
   ityāśayavānnityāparokṣaṃ bhagavantaṃ sambodhya stauti- niḥśeṣamiti //	iti-ASayavAn-nitya-aparokzam Bagavantam samboDya stOti niHSezam-iti //
   niḥśeṣadoṣarahitakalyāṇākhilasadguṇa /	niHSeza-doza-rahita-kalyANa-aKila-sat-guNaH /
   bhūtisvayambhuśarvādivandyaṃ tvāṃ naumi me priyam // MAnuv_4,4.14 //	BUti-svayamBu-Sarva-Adi-vandyam tvAm nOmi me priyam // Ma-anuv_4,4.14 //
   || iti śrīmadānandatīrthabhagavatpādācāryaviracite	|| iti SrImat-Ananda-tIrTa-Bagavat-pAda-AcArya-viracite
   śrīmadbrahmasūtrānuvyākhyāne caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ ||	SrImat-brahmasUtra-anuvyAKyAne caturTaH aDyAyaH ||
   NYĀYASUDHĀ:	NYĀYA-SUDHĀ:
   bhūtiḥ mahālakṣmīḥ /	BUtiH mahAlakzmIH /
   vacanaprasūnamālā jayatīrthākhyena bhikṣuṇā racitā /	vacana-prasUna-mAlA jayatIrTa-AKyena BikzuNA racitA /
   dhriyatāṃ hṛdaye sadaye kamalāmahilena pūruṣeṇa // 1 //	DriyatAm hRdaye sa-daye kamalA-mahilena pUruzeNa // 1 //
   na vaiduṣyabhrāntyā naca vacanacāturyakudhiyā na mātsaryāveśānnaca	na vEduzya-BrAntyA na-ca vacana-cAturya-ku-DiyA na mAtsarya-AveSAn-na-ca
   capalatādoṣavaśataḥ /	capalatA-doza-vaSataH /
   paraṃ śraddhājāḍyādakṛṣi kṛtimācāryavacasi skhalannapyetasmājjagati nahi	param SradDA-jAxyAt-akRzi kRtim-AcArI-avacasi sKalan=-api-etasmAt-jagati na-hi
   nindyo 'smi viduṣām // 2 //	nindyaH asmi viduzAm // 2 //
   anuvyākhyāmṛtāmbhodheḥ samutpannātinirmalā /	anuvyAKyA-amRta-amBoDeH samutpannA-ati-nirmalAH /
   iyaṃ nyāyasudhā bhaumairvibudhaiḥ sevyatāṃ sadā // 3 //	iyam nyAya-suDA BOmEH-vibuDEH sevyatAm sadA // 3 //
   iti śrīmatpūrṇapramatibhagavatpādasukṛteranuvyākhyānasya	iti SrImat-pUrNa-pramati-Bagavat-pAda-sukRteH-anuvyAKyAnasya
   praguṇajayatīrthākhyayatinā /	praguNa-jayatIrTa-AKyayatinA /
   kṛtāyāṃ ṭīkāyāṃ viṣamapadavākyārthavivṛtau caturthe 'dhyāye	kRtAyAm wIkAyAm vizama-pada-vAkya-arTa-vivRtO caturTe aDyAye
   'smiṃścaramacaraṇaḥ paryavasitaḥ // 4 //	asmin=-carama-caraNaH paryavasitaH // 4 //
